← Veg-Toon Studio / Facebook / Scripts 1–10

🎬 Ten shoot-ready 9:16 scripts · built on the competitor teardown · 14 July 2026

Facebook Scripts 1–10

Every scene numbered, every image prompt, every Veo 3 image-to-video prompt with its exact duration, and every line of dialogue with its timing inside the clip. Built to the envelope we measured off the winners — not to our old YouTube rules.

The shape, and why

10
scripts
78
shots to render
542s
total video (~9m 2s)
1207
Hindi words
4/6/8s
Veo 3 clip lengths only
Every rule below came out of the teardown, not out of my head. Clip lengths are 4, 6 or 8 seconds — never 10, because Veo 3.1 caps at 8s and the competitor built entirely from ~7.8s takes. Hindi is timed at 2.6 words/second, which is what the winners actually speak at. No dialogue line runs over 6 words. Dialogue starts within the first half-second and never stops — every one of the 5 competitor videos had zero silence gaps.
Render order. For each shot: (1) generate the keyframe image from the image prompt, (2) approve it, (3) feed that image + the image-to-video prompt into Veo 3 at the stated duration. The image prompt re-states every character's full design from scratch every single time — that is deliberate. It is the only thing that stops the vegetable drifting into a different vegetable between shots.
Two things to do in the edit, not in Veo. ① The PART 1 / COMMENT FOR NEXT PART / TAG KARO overlays are added in post (Canva/CapCut) — every prompt hard-bans on-screen text, because AI-rendered Devanagari comes out broken. ② Cover the bottom-right corner with our animated badge on every export. Two of the five competitors still have a generator watermark showing under their logo; Meta names visible third-party watermarks as an unoriginal-content trigger carrying a 90-day demonetisation.
Music. One continuous emotional score under the whole clip, no gaps. The prompts ask Veo for ambience + score, but replace it in the edit with a YouTube Audio Library / Pixabay bed — never NCS (Content-ID claims the revenue).

The ten

1. The Mother-in-Law Handed Her a Broom

सास ने बहू को झाड़ू थमाई

SERIAL · PART 1 64s · 9 shots 147 Hindi words OVERLAY: PART 1 END: COMMENT FOR NEXT PART NO MORAL

A saas showers her rich daughter-in-law with gold while stripping the poor one of every dignity, then threatens to throw her out unless the rest of the dowry arrives.

Why a scroller stops: The very first frame is a gold necklace being fastened on one bahu while the other stands barefoot with her head down — everyone knows exactly who is about to be destroyed.
Emotion arc: humiliation → helplessness → dread

Jamun जामुन · the saas, cruel and dowry-hungry Anaar अनार · the rich bahu, favoured, haughty Mooli मूली · the poor bahu, gentle, humiliated Aloo आलू · Mooli's husband, weak, kind

Scenes

SCENE 1.1 8s humiliation

Location: the marble-floored front room of a rich Indian village house, silk curtains, brass lamps, a wooden swing
Camera: medium wide, slow push in
Action: Jamun clasps a heavy gold necklace around Anaar's neck and turns her toward the light, admiring it. Mooli stands three steps away in a faded cotton saree, hands folded, head lowered. Jamun does not look at her once.

Time in clipWhoDialogue
0.4s – 2.8sJAMUNयह सोना मेरी असली बहू का।This gold belongs to my real daughter-in-law.
2.8s – 3.9sANAARशुक्रिया माँ जी।Thank you, mother-in-law.
3.9s – 5.9sJAMUNऔर तू? सिर झुका रह।And you? Keep your head down.
5.9s – 7.5sMOOLIमैंने कुछ नहीं माँगा।I never asked for anything.
Prompts for scene 1.1 — image + image-to-video (8s)
① IMAGE PROMPT — scene 1.1 keyframe
9:16 vertical. Photoreal 3D cinematic animation, Pixar-grade lighting and skin shading, shallow depth of field, film grain. Indian setting. Rich saturated Indian colour palette.

SCENE: the marble-floored front room of a rich Indian village house, silk curtains, brass lamps, a wooden swing

CHARACTER CONSTRUCTION (applies to every character in frame): each is a NORMAL ADULT HUMAN BODY with a real vegetable as the head. The vegetable forms the skull and face. Real HUMAN HAIR grows on top of the vegetable, and each has HUMAN eyes, HUMAN eyebrows, a HUMAN mouth and human skin-tone blush on the cheeks, set into the vegetable surface. They are NOT wearing masks, NOT costumes, NOT helmets — the vegetable IS the head. Everyone wears real Indian clothing on a real human body with real human hands.

CHARACTERS IN FRAME:
• JAMUN (black plum (jamun)) — a woman whose entire head is a single real JAMUN (Indian black plum) — deep blackish-purple glossy oval. Grey-streaked black human hair pulled into a tight bun. NOT a grape, NOT a brinjal, NOT a blueberry, NOT an olive. Wearing rich silk and gold — an embroidered silk saree with heavy gold jewellery.
• ANAAR (pomegranate) — a woman whose entire head is a single real POMEGRANATE — deep red, leathery skin, with the distinctive crown-shaped calyx on top. Black human hair coiled into an elaborate bun around the crown. NOT an apple, NOT a tomato, NOT a red ball, NOT a beetroot. Wearing rich silk and gold — an embroidered silk saree with heavy gold jewellery.
• MOOLI (white radish) — a woman whose entire head is a single real WHITE RADISH (mooli) — smooth pale ivory-white skin, long and tapering, with big leafy green radish tops sprouting from the crown. Long straight black human hair falling beside the radish. NOT a turnip, NOT a parsnip, NOT a white onion, NOT a daikon stub. Wearing a plain faded cotton saree, worn thin, no jewellery.

ACTION (frozen at this instant): Jamun clasps a heavy gold necklace around Anaar's neck and turns her toward the light, admiring it. Mooli stands three steps away in a faded cotton saree, hands folded, head lowered. Jamun does not look at her once.

CAMERA: medium wide, slow push in. MOOD: humiliation.

ABSOLUTELY NO text, no subtitles, no captions, no letters, no numbers, no watermark, no logo and no signage of any kind anywhere in the frame.
② IMAGE-TO-VIDEO PROMPT — scene 1.1 · Veo 3 · 8 seconds
Single continuous 8-second shot. 9:16 vertical. Animate the source image only.

RENDER LOCK: keep EXACTLY the characters from the source image (Jamun, Anaar, Mooli) — each keeps its exact vegetable head, human hair, human eyes and mouth, clothing and colours. NEVER turn them into ordinary humans, NEVER swap the vegetable for a different one, NEVER add or remove a character, NEVER change the wardrobe.

CAMERA: medium wide, slow push in.
[0s–0.4s] Jamun clasps a heavy gold necklace around Anaar's neck and turns her toward the light, admiring it.
DIALOGUE (Hindi, natural Indian village accent, lip-synced to the speaking mouth):
  [0.4s–2.8s] JAMUN says (Hindi): "यह सोना मेरी असली बहू का।"
  [2.8s–3.9s] ANAAR says (Hindi): "शुक्रिया माँ जी।"
  [3.9s–5.9s] JAMUN says (Hindi): "और तू? सिर झुका रह।"
  [5.9s–7.5s] MOOLI says (Hindi): "मैंने कुछ नहीं माँगा।"
[7.5s–8s] hold on the reaction.

LIP-SYNC LOCK: ONLY the character currently speaking moves their mouth. No overlapping speech.

AUDIO: the dialogue above, plus continuous room/street ambience and a soft emotional Indian background score under the whole clip — NO silence at any point.

ABSOLUTELY NO text, no subtitles, no captions, no letters, no numbers, no watermark, no logo and no signage of any kind anywhere in the frame.
SCENE 1.2 8s contempt

Location: the same rich front room, a wooden chest of dowry gifts open in the corner
Camera: medium, handheld, slight tilt down
Action: Jamun holds a thin paper envelope between two fingers, waves it in the air, then lets it drop. A few coins spill and roll across the marble. Mooli crouches to gather them. Jamun steps over the coins and walks past her.

Time in clipWhoDialogue
0.1s – 2.4sJAMUNतेरे बाप ने यह लिफ़ाफ़ा भेजा?Your father sent this envelope?
2.4s – 4.3sJAMUNपूरी उम्र की कमाई? हाँ?A whole life's earnings? Really?
4.3s – 5.9sMOOLIउन्होंने सब बेच दिया।He sold everything he had.
5.9s – 7.8sJAMUNअनार गाड़ी लेकर आई थी।Anaar arrived with a car.

SCENE 1.3 6s degradation

Location: the rich front room, doorway leading to a dim kitchen
Camera: low angle from floor level, then tilt up to Mooli's face
Action: Jamun tosses a broom; it clatters across the marble and stops against Mooli's bare feet. Mooli bends and picks it up slowly. Anaar watches from a silk chair, sipping tea, gold bangles glinting, saying nothing.

Time in clipWhoDialogue
0.1s – 2.0sJAMUNयह झाड़ू पकड़। आज से।Take this broom. From today.
2.0s – 4.0sJAMUNपूरा घर तू ही चमकाएगी।You alone will clean this house.
4.0s – 5.9sMOOLIमाँ जी, मैं कर लूँगी।Mother-in-law, I will do it.

SCENE 1.4 8s helplessness

Location: the rich front room, evening light through silk curtains
Camera: medium two-shot, slow push in on Jamun
Action: Aloo steps between his mother and his wife, palms open, his voice small. Jamun turns on him and he shrinks back half a step, eyes to the floor. Mooli's grip tightens on the broom handle. Anaar smirks behind her teacup.

Time in clipWhoDialogue
0.3s – 2.2sALOOमाँ, मूली भी बहू है।Mother, Mooli is a daughter-in-law too.
2.2s – 4.1sJAMUNचुप! तुझे कौन पूछ रहा?Quiet! Who asked you?
4.1s – 6.1sALOOमाँ, यह ठीक नहीं है।Mother, this is not right.
6.1s – 7.6sJAMUNदहेज लाई है यह?Did she bring any dowry?

SCENE 1.5 4s mockery

Location: the rich front room, silk chair, warm lamp light
Camera: tight on Anaar's wrist, then snap up to her face
Action: Anaar rolls a thick stack of gold bangles slowly down her forearm so they chime, then throws her head back and laughs, the gold catching the lamplight across her face.

Time in clipWhoDialogue
0.4s – 2.0sANAARगरीब घर की बहू।A daughter-in-law from a poor house.
2.0s – 3.5sANAARमेरे कंगन तो गिन।Go on, count my bangles.

SCENE 1.6 8s dread

Location: a dim smoke-stained kitchen at night, one bare bulb, a stone sink
Camera: medium wide, slow push in past the dishes
Action: Jamun points at a mountain of greasy steel plates, pots and glasses stacked over the stone sink. Mooli's cracked hands hover above the cold grey water. Jamun folds her arms in the doorway and does not move.

Time in clipWhoDialogue
0.4s – 2.4sJAMUNयह जूठे बर्तन देख ले।Look at these dirty dishes.
2.4s – 4.3sJAMUNसुबह तक सब चमकने चाहिए।All of them shining by morning.
4.3s – 6.3sMOOLIमेरे हाथ काँप रहे हैं।My hands are shaking.
6.3s – 7.5sJAMUNबहाने मत बना।Don't make excuses.

2. One Hand, Two Lives

एक हाथ, दो जानें

TAG / COMMENT BAIT 42s · 8 shots 97 Hindi words END: TAG KARO APNE BESTY KO NO MORAL

When a rope bridge gives way, Aloo dangles holding his childhood best friend in one hand and the woman he loves in the other — he can only save one, and he picks his friend without a second of regret.

Why a scroller stops: Frame one is a man hanging over a gorge with two screaming people in his fists — the scroller has to know which one he drops.
Emotion arc: panic → impossible choice → betrayal → shameless warmth → direct provocation

Aloo आलू · the hero hanging from the broken bridge Baingan बैंगन · his childhood best friend Gajar गाजर · the woman he loves

Scenes

SCENE 2.1 4s panic

Location: a snapped rope bridge over a deep rocky gorge, white river far below, mist and swinging frayed ropes
Camera: wide, camera swinging with the bridge, handheld
Action: The rope bridge has already given way. Aloo hangs from a splintered plank, knees hooked over wood, one fist clamped on Baingan's wrist and the other on Gajar's wrist. Both swing freely above the gorge. Ropes fray and pop above him.

Time in clipWhoDialogue
0.1s – 2.0sALOOहाथ मत छोड़ना! पकड़े रहो!Don't let go! Hold on!
2.0s – 3.9sBAINGANआलू! मैं गिर रहा हूँ!Aloo! I'm falling!

• ALOO (potato) — a man whose entire head is a single large real POTATO — earthy light-brown skin, shallow eye-dents, faint soil speckles, irregular lumpy shape. Thick black human hair combed back on top of the potato. NOT a sweet potato, NOT a smooth ball, NOT a stone, NOT a round dumpling. Wearing a plain faded cotton kurta and worn sandals.
• BAINGAN (brinjal (eggplant)) — a man whose entire head is a single real BRINJAL — deep glossy dark-purple teardrop with a green star-shaped calyx crown on top. Black human hair swept under the calyx. NOT a plum, NOT a fig, NOT a grape, NOT a black berry. Wearing a plain faded cotton kurta and worn sandals.
• GAJAR (carrot) — a woman whose entire head is a single real CARROT — bright orange, tapering, with faint horizontal ridges, and feathery green carrot fronds sprouting on top. Long black human hair braided below the fronds. NOT a chilli, NOT a sweet potato, NOT an orange cone, NOT a pumpkin. Wearing a plain faded cotton saree, worn thin, no jewellery.

ACTION (frozen at this instant): The rope bridge has already given way. Aloo hangs from a splintered plank, knees hooked over wood, one fist clamped on Baingan's wrist and the other on Gajar's wrist. Both swing freely above the gorge. Ropes fray and pop above him.

CAMERA: wide, camera swinging with the bridge, handheld. MOOD: panic.

3. Sixty Days, Sixty Onions

साठ दिन, साठ प्याज़

WARM · HAS A MORAL 32s · 4 shots 74 Hindi words HAS A MORAL

An onion-seller finally works out why the potato man has bought onions from her stall every single day for sixty days — and he confesses.

Why a scroller stops: A woman is publicly tearing into a shy customer over a bag of onions, and the whole market is watching — you have to know what he did.
Emotion arc: irritation → suspicion → realisation → warmth

Pyaaz प्याज़ · the onion-seller who runs the stall Aloo आलू · the shy daily customer Nimbu नींबू · the mischievous neighbouring stallholder

Scenes

SCENE 3.1 8s public irritation

Location: a crowded sabzi mandi lane in morning light, sacks of onions, hanging marigold strings, tin roofs, shoppers pressing past
Camera: medium wide across the stall, slow push in
Action: Pyaaz slams a brass weight onto her scale and glares across the stall at Aloo, who clutches a small cloth bag of onions. Shoppers turn to stare at him. Nimbu leans over from the next stall, grinning, chewing a stalk.

Time in clipWhoDialogue
0.4s – 2.0sPYAAZरोज़ क्यों आते हो?Why do you come every day?
2.0s – 3.2sALOOप्याज़ चाहिए, बस।I need onions, that's all.
3.2s – 4.7sPYAAZकल भी यही कहा।You said the same yesterday.
4.7s – 6.3sNIMBUपूरा बाज़ार हँस रहा।The whole market is laughing.
6.3s – 7.5sALOOचुप रहो, नींबू।Be quiet, Nimbu.
Prompts for scene 3.1 — image + image-to-video (8s)
① IMAGE PROMPT — scene 3.1 keyframe
9:16 vertical. Photoreal 3D cinematic animation, Pixar-grade lighting and skin shading, shallow depth of field, film grain. Indian setting. Rich saturated Indian colour palette.

SCENE: a crowded sabzi mandi lane in morning light, sacks of onions, hanging marigold strings, tin roofs, shoppers pressing past

CHARACTER CONSTRUCTION (applies to every character in frame): each is a NORMAL ADULT HUMAN BODY with a real vegetable as the head. The vegetable forms the skull and face. Real HUMAN HAIR grows on top of the vegetable, and each has HUMAN eyes, HUMAN eyebrows, a HUMAN mouth and human skin-tone blush on the cheeks, set into the vegetable surface. They are NOT wearing masks, NOT costumes, NOT helmets — the vegetable IS the head. Everyone wears real Indian clothing on a real human body with real human hands.

CHARACTERS IN FRAME:
• PYAAZ (onion) — a woman whose entire head is a single real ONION — glossy pink-purple bulb with fine papery skin layers and a small green shoot on top. Black human hair in a long braid. NOT garlic, NOT a shallot, NOT a beetroot, NOT a pink ball. Wearing a plain faded cotton saree, worn thin, no jewellery.
• ALOO (potato) — a man whose entire head is a single large real POTATO — earthy light-brown skin, shallow eye-dents, faint soil speckles, irregular lumpy shape. Thick black human hair combed back on top of the potato. NOT a sweet potato, NOT a smooth ball, NOT a stone, NOT a round dumpling. Wearing a plain faded cotton kurta and worn sandals.
• NIMBU (lemon) — a man whose entire head is a single real LEMON — bright yellow, dimpled peel, small nub at the tip. Messy black human hair. NOT an orange, NOT a mango, NOT a lime, NOT a yellow ball. Wearing a plain faded cotton kurta and worn sandals.

ACTION (frozen at this instant): Pyaaz slams a brass weight onto her scale and glares across the stall at Aloo, who clutches a small cloth bag of onions. Shoppers turn to stare at him. Nimbu leans over from the next stall, grinning, chewing a stalk.

CAMERA: medium wide across the stall, slow push in. MOOD: public irritation.

SCENE 3.2 8s suspicion

Location: the same sabzi mandi stall, onion sacks piled high, dust in the sunbeams, a crowd gathering closer
Camera: medium, slow arc around the stall
Action: Nimbu jumps down and points at Aloo's empty cloth bag. Pyaaz steps out from behind her onion sacks, the brass weight still in her hand, her glare sliding into confusion. Aloo backs into a hanging string of marigolds, eyes down.

Time in clipWhoDialogue
0.4s – 2.0sNIMBUये प्याज़ खाता नहीं।He doesn't even eat the onions.
2.0s – 3.6sPYAAZफिर रोज़ क्यों खरीदता?Then why does he buy daily?
3.6s – 5.1sNIMBUसब मंदिर में बाँटता।He gives them all to the temple.
5.1s – 6.3sPYAAZसच बोलो, आलू।Tell the truth, Aloo.
6.3s – 7.5sALOOबस… रहने दो।Please… let it go.

Real HUMAN HAIR grows on top of the vegetable, and each has HUMAN eyes, HUMAN eyebrows, a HUMAN mouth and human skin-tone blush on the cheeks, set into the vegetable surface. They are NOT wearing masks, NOT costumes, NOT helmets — the vegetable IS the head. Everyone wears real Indian clothing on a real human body with real human hands.

CHARACTERS IN FRAME:
• PYAAZ (onion) — a woman whose entire head is a single real ONION — glossy pink-purple bulb with fine papery skin layers and a small green shoot on top. Black human hair in a long braid. NOT garlic, NOT a shallot, NOT a beetroot, NOT a pink ball. Wearing a plain faded cotton saree, worn thin, no jewellery.
• ALOO (potato) — a man whose entire head is a single large real POTATO — earthy light-brown skin, shallow eye-dents, faint soil speckles, irregular lumpy shape. Thick black human hair combed back on top of the potato. NOT a sweet potato, NOT a smooth ball, NOT a stone, NOT a round dumpling. Wearing a plain faded cotton kurta and worn sandals.
• NIMBU (lemon) — a man whose entire head is a single real LEMON — bright yellow, dimpled peel, small nub at the tip. Messy black human hair. NOT an orange, NOT a mango, NOT a lime, NOT a yellow ball. Wearing a plain faded cotton kurta and worn sandals.

ACTION (frozen at this instant): Pyaaz slams a brass weight onto her scale and glares across the stall at Aloo, who clutches a small cloth bag of onions. Shoppers turn to stare at him. Nimbu leans over from the next stall, grinning, chewing a stalk.

CAMERA: medium wide across the stall, slow push in. MOOD: public irritation.

4. The Son Who Came Back After Twenty Years

बीस साल बाद बेटा लौटा

VILLAIN WINS 76s · 10 shots 169 Hindi words NO MORAL

A schemer dresses up a look-alike young man as a rich couple's long-lost son, and once the mother has wept with joy and taken him in, he empties their safe and vanishes — while they go on shopping for him.

Why a scroller stops: The very first frame is a man being painted with a fake birthmark — you instantly know a lie is being built, and you have to see who it lands on.
Emotion arc: greed → false joy → dramatic irony → betrayal → dread

Tamatar टमाटर · the ruthless schemer who builds the con Nimbu नींबू · the lean young man passed off as the lost son Shimla शिमला मिर्च · the rich, smug father Anaar अनार · the rich, haughty mother who lost her son

Scenes

SCENE 4.1 8s cold scheming

Location: a cramped back-alley room at dusk, cracked mirror, oil lamp, a borrowed silk kurta hanging on a nail
Camera: medium close, slow push in on the mirror reflection
Action: Tamatar grips the jaw of Nimbu, a lean young man, and smears a dark birthmark onto his neck with a charcoal stub. Nimbu practises a trembling, tearful face in the cracked mirror. Tamatar shakes his head and corrects the expression, hard.

Time in clipWhoDialogue
0.1s – 1.6sTAMATARरो मत, बस काँप।Don't cry, just tremble.

5. His File, Her Interview

उसकी फ़ाइल, उसका इंटरव्यू

KARMA FLIP 56s · 8 shots 129 Hindi words NO MORAL

A rich pomegranate woman throws a poor okra helper's file on the floor in front of the whole office; years later she walks into a job interview and the calm, polite man behind the desk is him.

Why a scroller stops: The first frame is papers flying and a rich woman screaming at a man on his knees — you have to know what he did.
Emotion arc: humiliation → silent endurance → dread → collapse

Anaar अनार · the rich, haughty young woman Bhindi भिंडी · the poor office helper, later the manager Shimla शिमला मिर्च · her smug rich colleague Pyaaz प्याज़ · the old office woman, later the receptionist

Scenes

SCENE 5.1 8s humiliation

Location: a shabby old office corridor, peeling paint, tube lights, a crowd of staff pressed against the walls
Camera: medium wide, handheld, slow push in
Action: Anaar in a heavy silk saree and gold flings a paper file at the floor; loose pages skid across the tiles. Bhindi, thin, in faded cotton, stands frozen with his hands still open. The staff crowd stares and murmurs. Shimla smirks beside her.

Time in clipWhoDialogue
0.3s – 2.6sANAARयह कचरा मेरे सामने मत लाओ।Don't bring this garbage in front of me.
2.6s – 4.1sBHINDIमैडम, फ़ाइल तैयार है।Madam, the file is ready.
4.1s – 6.1sANAARफ़ाइल? तेरी औकात क्या है?File? What is your worth?
6.1s – 7.6sSHIMLAमैडम, इसे बाहर करवाइए।Madam, have him thrown out.

6. He Called His Mother The Maid

माँ नहीं, नौकरानी कह दिया

TAG / COMMENT BAIT 56s · 8 shots 117 Hindi words END: TAG KARO APNE MAA KO NO MORAL

A poor mother brings her son's lunch tin to his rich college, he denies her in front of his friends and calls her the maid, and only after she leaves does he find the pawn receipt for her last gold bangles folded inside the tin.

Why a scroller stops: The first frame is two rich students openly laughing at a mother's torn saree while her own son stands there saying nothing.
Emotion arc: humiliation → denial → silent devastation → unbearable guilt

Aloo आलू · the ashamed son, a student Mooli मूली · his poor mother Shimla शिमला मिर्च · rich college friend, smug Anaar अनार · rich college friend, haughty

Scenes

SCENE 6.1 8s humiliation

Location: a bright modern college corridor, glass doors, polished floor, glossy notice boards
Camera: medium wide, slow push in past the two rich students toward the doorway
Action: Shimla and Anaar lean on a glass door in silk and gold, laughing and pointing at Mooli, who stands just inside the entrance in a faded worn saree and cracked slippers, clutching a dented steel lunch tin against her chest. Aloo stands frozen between them, jaw tight, eyes on the floor.

Time in clipWhoDialogue
0.1s – 2.4sSHIMLAये कौन है? भिखारन लगती है।Who is this? She looks like a beggar.
2.4s – 4.3sANAARकैसी फटी साड़ी पहनी है!What a torn saree she's wearing!
4.3s – 6.3sSHIMLAआलू, ये तेरे यहाँ क्यों?Aloo, why is she here for you?
6.3s – 7.8sMOOLIबेटा, टिफ़िन लाई हूँ।Son, I brought your lunch tin.
Prompts for scene 6.1 — image + image-to-video (8s)
① IMAGE PROMPT — scene 6.1 keyframe
9:16 vertical. Photoreal 3D cinematic animation, Pixar-grade lighting and skin shading, shallow depth of field, film grain. Indian setting. Rich saturated Indian colour palette.

SCENE: a bright modern college corridor, glass doors, polished floor, glossy notice boards

CHARACTER CONSTRUCTION (applies to every character in frame): each is a NORMAL ADULT HUMAN BODY with a real vegetable as the head. The vegetable forms the skull and face. Real HUMAN HAIR grows on top of the vegetable, and each has HUMAN eyes, HUMAN eyebrows, a HUMAN mouth and human skin-tone blush on the cheeks, set into the vegetable surface. They are NOT wearing masks, NOT costumes, NOT helmets — the vegetable IS the head. Everyone wears real Indian clothing on a real human body with real human hands.

CHARACTERS IN FRAME:
• ALOO (potato) — a man whose entire head is a single large real POTATO — earthy light-brown skin, shallow eye-dents, faint soil speckles, irregular lumpy shape. Thick black human hair combed back on top of the potato. NOT a sweet potato, NOT a smooth ball, NOT a stone, NOT a round dumpling. Wearing a plain faded cotton kurta and worn sandals.
• MOOLI (white radish) — a woman whose entire head is a single real WHITE RADISH (mooli) — smooth pale ivory-white skin, long and tapering, with big leafy green radish tops sprouting from the crown. Long straight black human hair falling beside the radish. NOT a turnip, NOT a parsnip, NOT a white onion, NOT a daikon stub. Wearing a plain faded cotton saree, worn thin, no jewellery.
• SHIMLA (bell pepper) — a man whose entire head is a single real BELL PEPPER (shimla mirch) — glossy, blocky, deeply lobed, with a thick green stem on top. Oiled black human hair parted at the side. NOT a chilli, NOT a tomato, NOT an apple, NOT a smooth green ball. Wearing a rich silk kurta with gold rings and an embroidered waistcoat.
• ANAAR (pomegranate) — a woman whose entire head is a single real POMEGRANATE — deep red, leathery skin, with the distinctive crown-shaped calyx on top. Black human hair coiled into an elaborate bun around the crown. NOT an apple, NOT a tomato, NOT a red ball, NOT a beetroot. Wearing rich silk and gold — an embroidered silk saree with heavy gold jewellery.

ACTION (frozen at this instant): Shimla and Anaar lean on a glass door in silk and gold, laughing and pointing at Mooli, who stands just inside the entrance in a faded worn saree and cracked slippers, clutching a dented steel lunch tin against her chest. Aloo stands frozen between them, jaw tight, eyes on the floor.

CAMERA: medium wide, slow push in past the two rich students toward the doorway. MOOD: humiliation.

SCENE 6.2 8s denial

Location: the same college corridor, sunlight cutting across the polished floor
Camera: medium two-shot on Aloo, then a small step back to include the laughing friends
Action: Aloo turns his back half away from Mooli and speaks to his friends instead of to her, waving a dismissive hand toward the doorway without looking at her. Shimla doubles over laughing. Anaar smirks and flicks her gold bangles. Mooli's arms tighten around the tin.

===== SCENE 6.1 — IMAGE =====
9:16 vertical. Photoreal 3D cinematic animation, Pixar-grade lighting and skin shading, shallow depth of field, film grain. Indian setting. Rich saturated Indian colour palette.

SCENE: a bright modern college corridor, glass doors, polished floor, glossy notice boards

CHARACTER CONSTRUCTION (applies to every character in frame): each is a NORMAL ADULT HUMAN BODY with a real vegetable as the head. The vegetable forms the skull and face. Real HUMAN HAIR grows on top of the vegetable, and each has HUMAN eyes, HUMAN eyebrows, a HUMAN mouth and human skin-tone blush on the cheeks, set into the vegetable surface. They are NOT wearing masks, NOT costumes, NOT helmets — the vegetable IS the head. Everyone wears real Indian clothing on a real human body with real human hands.

CHARACTERS IN FRAME:
• ALOO (potato) — a man whose entire head is a single large real POTATO — earthy light-brown skin, shallow eye-dents, faint soil speckles, irregular lumpy shape. Thick black human hair combed back on top of the potato. NOT a sweet potato, NOT a smooth ball, NOT a stone, NOT a round dumpling. Wearing a plain faded cotton kurta and worn sandals.
• MOOLI (white radish) — a woman whose entire head is a single real WHITE RADISH (mooli) — smooth pale ivory-white skin, long and tapering, with big leafy green radish tops sprouting from the crown. Long straight black human hair falling beside the radish. NOT a turnip, NOT a parsnip, NOT a white onion, NOT a daikon stub. Wearing a plain faded cotton saree, worn thin, no jewellery.
• SHIMLA (bell pepper) — a man whose entire head is a single real BELL PEPPER (shimla mirch) — glossy, blocky, deeply lobed, with a thick green stem on top. Oiled black human hair parted at the side. NOT a chilli, NOT a tomato, NOT an apple, NOT a smooth green ball. Wearing a rich silk kurta with gold rings and an embroidered waistcoat.
• ANAAR (pomegranate) — a woman whose entire head is a single real POMEGRANATE — deep red, leathery skin, with the distinctive crown-shaped calyx on top. Black human hair coiled into an elaborate bun around the crown. NOT an apple, NOT a tomato, NOT a red ball, NOT a beetroot. Wearing rich silk and gold — an embroidered silk saree with heavy gold jewellery.

ACTION (frozen at this instant): Shimla and Anaar lean on a glass door in silk and gold, laughing and pointing at Mooli, who stands just inside the entrance in a faded worn saree and cracked slippers, clutching a dented steel lunch tin against her chest. Aloo stands frozen between them, jaw tight, eyes on the floor.

CAMERA: medium wide, slow push in past the two rich students toward the doorway. MOOD: humiliation.

ABSOLUTELY NO text, no subtitles, no captions, no letters, no numbers, no watermark, no logo and no signage of any kind anywhere in the frame.

7. One Plate of Food

एक थाली खाना

KARMA FLIP 48s · 7 shots 103 Hindi words NO MORAL

A rich sweet-shop owner mocks a starving labourer at his door; the night a storm burns the market down, the same labourer is the only one who brings him a plate of food.

Why a scroller stops: The very first frame is a starving man's hand being laughed at by a rich man in front of his paying customers.
Emotion arc: humiliation → quiet kindness → ruin → reversal → shame

Bhindi भिंडी · the starving day-labourer Shimla शिमला मिर्च · the rich sweet-shop owner Aloo आलू · the poor chaiwala across the street

Scenes

SCENE 7.1 8s humiliation

Location: the marble step of a glittering sweet-shop in a busy Indian market, glass trays of mithai, evening lights
Camera: medium wide, slow push in past the customers
Action: Outside a glittering sweet-shop, thin dust-covered Bhindi holds out a trembling empty hand toward Shimla, who stands on the marble step in silk and gold, smirking at his seated customers. They laugh into their plates. Bhindi's shoulders sink.

Time in clipWhoDialogue
0.3s – 2.6sBHINDIसाहब, दो दिन से भूखा हूँ।Sir, I have been hungry two days.
2.6s – 4.1sSHIMLAयह दुकान है, भिखारी।This is a shop, beggar.
4.1s – 6.1sSHIMLAखाना पैसे से मिलता है।Food comes with money.
6.1s – 7.6sBHINDIबस थोड़ा सा, साहब।Just a little, sir.

• SHIMLA (bell pepper) — a man whose entire head is a single real BELL PEPPER (shimla mirch) — glossy, blocky, deeply lobed, with a thick green stem on top. Oiled black human hair parted at the side. NOT a chilli, NOT a tomato, NOT an apple, NOT a smooth green ball. Wearing a rich silk kurta with gold rings and an embroidered waistcoat.

8. The Garland Went to Another Neck

जयमाला किसी और के गले

SERIAL · PART 1 64s · 9 shots 138 Hindi words OVERLAY: PART 1 END: COMMENT FOR NEXT PART NO MORAL

On his wedding day, Aloo's bride Gajar walks past him at the mandap and garlands the rich Shimla instead, leaving Aloo alone holding his own jaimala.

Why a scroller stops: The first frame is a bride walking past her groom mid-ceremony to garland another man — the humiliation is already happening before you can scroll.
Emotion arc: disbelief → public humiliation → rage → abandonment

Aloo आलू · the poor groom, honest and hardworking Gajar गाजर · the bride who betrays him Shimla शिमला मिर्च · the rich, smug rival Tamatar टमाटर · Aloo's loud, loyal friend

Scenes

SCENE 8.1 8s public humiliation

Location: a village wedding mandap at dusk, four flower-wrapped poles, marigold strings, a small sacred fire, rows of plastic chairs full of guests
Camera: medium wide, slow push in
Action: Gajar in a red bridal saree walks down the aisle holding a jaimala. She passes Aloo without a glance and lowers the garland over Shimla's neck. Aloo stands frozen mid-ceremony, his own garland still raised in both hands. Tamatar half-rises from his chair.

• GAJAR (carrot) — a woman whose entire head is a single real CARROT — bright orange, tapering, with faint horizontal ridges, and feathery green carrot fronds sprouting on top. Long black human hair braided below the fronds. NOT a chilli, NOT a sweet potato, NOT an orange cone, NOT a pumpkin. Wearing a plain faded cotton saree, worn thin, no jewellery.
• TAMATAR (tomato) — a man whose entire head is a single real TOMATO — bright glossy red, perfectly round, a small green star calyx on top. Black human hair around the calyx. NOT an apple, NOT a capsicum, NOT a cherry, NOT a red ball. Wearing a plain faded cotton kurta and worn sandals.

===== SCENE 8.1 — IMAGE =====
9:16 vertical. Photoreal 3D cinematic animation, Pixar-grade lighting and skin shading, shallow depth of field, film grain. Indian setting. Rich saturated Indian colour palette.

SCENE: a village wedding mandap at dusk, four flower-wrapped poles, marigold strings, a small sacred fire, rows of plastic chairs full of guests

CHARACTER CONSTRUCTION (applies to every character in frame): each is a NORMAL ADULT HUMAN BODY with a real vegetable as the head. The vegetable forms the skull and face. Real HUMAN HAIR grows on top of the vegetable, and each has HUMAN eyes, HUMAN eyebrows, a HUMAN mouth and human skin-tone blush on the cheeks, set into the vegetable surface. They are NOT wearing masks, NOT costumes, NOT helmets — the vegetable IS the head. Everyone wears real Indian clothing on a real human body with real human hands.

CHARACTERS IN FRAME:
• ALOO (potato) — a man whose entire head is a single large real POTATO — earthy light-brown skin, shallow eye-dents, faint soil speckles, irregular lumpy shape. Thick black human hair combed back on top of the potato. NOT a sweet potato, NOT a smooth ball, NOT a stone, NOT a round dumpling. Wearing a plain faded cotton kurta and worn sandals.
• GAJAR (carrot) — a woman whose entire head is a single real CARROT — bright orange, tapering, with faint horizontal ridges, and feathery green carrot fronds sprouting on top. Long black human hair braided below the fronds. NOT a chilli, NOT a sweet potato, NOT an orange cone, NOT a pumpkin. Wearing a plain faded cotton saree, worn thin, no jewellery.
• SHIMLA (bell pepper) — a man whose entire head is a single real BELL PEPPER (shimla mirch) — glossy, blocky, deeply lobed, with a thick green stem on top. Oiled black human hair parted at the side. NOT a chilli, NOT a tomato, NOT an apple, NOT a smooth green ball. Wearing a rich silk kurta with gold rings and an embroidered waistcoat.
• TAMATAR (tomato) — a man whose entire head is a single real TOMATO — bright glossy red, perfectly round, a small green star calyx on top. Black human hair around the calyx. NOT an apple, NOT a capsicum, NOT a cherry, NOT a red ball. Wearing a plain faded cotton kurta and worn sandals.

ACTION (frozen at this instant): Gajar in a red bridal saree walks down the aisle holding a jaimala. She passes Aloo without a glance and lowers the garland over Shimla's neck. Aloo stands frozen mid-ceremony, his own garland still raised in both hands. Tamatar half-rises from his chair.

CAMERA: medium wide, slow push in. MOOD: public humiliation.

ABSOLUTELY NO text, no subtitles, no captions, no letters, no numbers, no watermark, no logo and no signage of any kind anywhere in the frame.

9. Dividing Up Mother

माँ का बँटवारा

TAG / COMMENT BAIT 48s · 7 shots 110 Hindi words END: COMMENT KARO — KAUN SAHI HAI? NO MORAL

Two grown sons argue in a courtyard over who must take their widowed mother — the rich one offers money instead of a room, the poor one offers a room he can barely afford — while she stands silently between them holding her bundle.

Why a scroller stops: The first frame is a rich son and a poor son haggling over an old woman who is standing right there, holding her belongings, saying nothing.
Emotion arc: haggling → invisibility → quiet dignity → provocation

Jamun जामुन · the old widowed mother, frail and silent Aloo आलू · the poor son with a tiny home Shimla शिमला मिर्च · the rich son with a big house Pyaaz प्याज़ · the neighbour watching from the gate

Scenes

SCENE 9.1 8s argument in progress

Location: a cracked mud-brick courtyard at midday, a big painted house on one side, brass pots, dust
Camera: medium wide, slow push in
Action: Shimla, in silk kurta and gold rings, jabs a finger toward Aloo, who stands in faded cotton with his hands open. Between them their old mother Jamun stands completely still, a small cloth bundle clutched against her chest, eyes lowered.

Time in clipWhoDialogue
0.4s – 2.4sSHIMLAमेरे घर में जगह नहीं।There is no room in my house.
2.4s – 4.3sALOOतेरा घर महल जैसा है।Your house is like a palace.
4.3s – 5.9sSHIMLAकमरे भरे हुए हैं।The rooms are all full.
5.9s – 7.5sALOOमाँ के लिए नहीं?Not for mother?
Prompts for scene 9.1 — image + image-to-video (8s)
① IMAGE PROMPT — scene 9.1 keyframe
9:16 vertical. Photoreal 3D cinematic animation, Pixar-grade lighting and skin shading, shallow depth of field, film grain. Indian setting. Rich saturated Indian colour palette.

SCENE: a cracked mud-brick courtyard at midday, a big painted house on one side, brass pots, dust

CHARACTER CONSTRUCTION (applies to every character in frame): each is a NORMAL ADULT HUMAN BODY with a real vegetable as the head. The vegetable forms the skull and face. Real HUMAN HAIR grows on top of the vegetable, and each has HUMAN eyes, HUMAN eyebrows, a HUMAN mouth and human skin-tone blush on the cheeks, set into the vegetable surface. They are NOT wearing masks, NOT costumes, NOT helmets — the vegetable IS the head. Everyone wears real Indian clothing on a real human body with real human hands.

CHARACTERS IN FRAME:
• JAMUN (black plum (jamun)) — a woman whose entire head is a single real JAMUN (Indian black plum) — deep blackish-purple glossy oval. Grey-streaked black human hair pulled into a tight bun. NOT a grape, NOT a brinjal, NOT a blueberry, NOT an olive. Wearing a plain faded cotton saree, worn thin, no jewellery.
• ALOO (potato) — a man whose entire head is a single large real POTATO — earthy light-brown skin, shallow eye-dents, faint soil speckles, irregular lumpy shape. Thick black human hair combed back on top of the potato. NOT a sweet potato, NOT a smooth ball, NOT a stone, NOT a round dumpling. Wearing a plain faded cotton kurta and worn sandals.
• SHIMLA (bell pepper) — a man whose entire head is a single real BELL PEPPER (shimla mirch) — glossy, blocky, deeply lobed, with a thick green stem on top. Oiled black human hair parted at the side. NOT a chilli, NOT a tomato, NOT an apple, NOT a smooth green ball. Wearing a rich silk kurta with gold rings and an embroidered waistcoat.

ACTION (frozen at this instant): Shimla, in silk kurta and gold rings, jabs a finger toward Aloo, who stands in faded cotton with his hands open. Between them their old mother Jamun stands completely still, a small cloth bundle clutched against her chest, eyes lowered.

CAMERA: medium wide, slow push in. MOOD: argument in progress.

10. House of Silver, Bride of Clay

चाँदी का घर, मिट्टी की बहू

SERIAL · PART 1 56s · 8 shots 123 Hindi words OVERLAY: PART 1 END: COMMENT FOR NEXT PART NO MORAL

A rich family of mirror-chrome vegetables tells their son's poor matte bride that she will never be one of them, and hands her a tin of silver polish to fix herself.

Why a scroller stops: An entire family rendered in gleaming liquid chrome, and one dull ordinary bride sitting among them who reflects nothing — the frame itself is the insult, and nobody has seen this look on a veg cartoon before.
Emotion arc: humiliation → isolation → self-doubt → unresolved dread

Anaar अनार · CHROME — the haughty rich mother-in-law Jamun जामुन · CHROME — the severe elder matriarch Shimla शिमला मिर्च · CHROME — the rich smug husband Mooli मूली · MATTE — the poor bride, reflects no light

Scenes

SCENE 10.1 8s humiliation

Location: a vast marble dining hall at night, long table, blazing candelabra, mirror-polished floor
Camera: medium wide, slow push in
Action: A long marble dining hall, candles blazing. Anaar's chrome hand points a mirror-bright finger across the table at Mooli, whose radish head is dull matte white. Jamun, also chrome, watches, unmoving.

Time in clipWhoDialogue
0.1s – 2.0sANAARतुम चमकती ही नहीं हो।You simply do not shine.
2.0s – 4.0sANAARहमारे जैसी कभी नहीं बनोगी।You will never become one of us.
4.0s – 5.9sMOOLIमाँ जी, मैं कोशिश करूँगी।Mother-in-law, I will try.
5.9s – 7.8sJAMUNकोशिश से चमक नहीं आती।Trying does not bring shine.

CHARACTERS IN FRAME:
• ANAAR (pomegranate) — a woman whose entire head is a single real POMEGRANATE — deep red, leathery skin, with the distinctive crown-shaped calyx on top. Black human hair coiled into an elaborate bun around the crown. NOT an apple, NOT a tomato, NOT a red ball, NOT a beetroot. Wearing rich silk and gold — an embroidered silk saree with heavy gold jewellery. • MOOLI (white radish) — a woman whose entire head is a single real WHITE RADISH (mooli) — smooth pale ivory-white skin, long and tapering, with big leafy green radish tops sprouting from the crown. Long straight black human hair falling beside the radish. NOT a turnip, NOT a parsnip, NOT a white onion, NOT a daikon stub. Wearing a plain faded cotton saree, worn thin, no jewellery. IN DELIBERATE CONTRAST TO THE CHROME FAMILY: rendered in ordinary MATTE organic material — dull, soft, porous, light-absorbing skin and rough homespun cloth. She casts NO reflection, throws NO highlight, and does not appear in the mirrored floor or in any polished surface.

Prompts for scene 10.2 — image + image-to-video (8s)
① IMAGE PROMPT — scene 10.2 keyframe
9:16 vertical. Photoreal 3D cinematic animation, Pixar-grade lighting and skin shading, shallow depth of field, film grain. Indian setting. Rich saturated Indian colour palette.

SCENE: the same marble dining hall, chandelier overhead

CHARACTER CONSTRUCTION (applies to every character in frame): each is a NORMAL ADULT HUMAN BODY with a real vegetable as the head. The vegetable forms the skull and face. Real HUMAN HAIR grows on top of the vegetable, and each has HUMAN eyes, HUMAN eyebrows, a HUMAN mouth and human skin-tone blush on the cheeks, set into the vegetable surface. They are NOT wearing masks, NOT costumes, NOT helmets — the vegetable IS the head. Everyone wears real Indian clothing on a real human body with real human hands.

CHARACTERS IN FRAME:
• ANAAR (pomegranate) — a woman whose entire head is a single real POMEGRANATE — deep red, leathery skin, with the distinctive crown-shaped calyx on top. Black human hair coiled into an elaborate bun around the crown. NOT an apple, NOT a tomato, NOT a red ball, NOT a beetroot. Wearing rich silk and gold — an embroidered silk saree with heavy gold jewellery. RENDERED ENTIRELY IN POLISHED LIQUID CHROME — mirror-finish metallic silver skin, hair and clothing, reflecting the room like a mirror. The vegetable shape is unchanged, only the material is chrome.
• JAMUN (black plum (jamun)) — a woman whose entire head is a single real JAMUN (Indian black plum) — deep blackish-purple glossy oval. Grey-streaked black human hair pulled into a tight bun. NOT a grape, NOT a brinjal, NOT a blueberry, NOT an olive. Wearing rich silk and gold — an embroidered silk saree with heavy gold jewellery. RENDERED ENTIRELY IN POLISHED LIQUID CHROME — mirror-finish metallic silver skin, hair and clothing, reflecting the room like a mirror. The vegetable shape is unchanged, only the material is chrome.
• SHIMLA (bell pepper) — a man whose entire head is a single real BELL PEPPER (shimla mirch) — glossy, blocky, deeply lobed, with a thick green stem on top. Oiled black human hair parted at the side. NOT a chilli, NOT a tomato, NOT an apple, NOT a smooth green ball. Wearing a rich silk kurta with gold rings and an embroidered waistcoat. RENDERED ENTIRELY IN POLISHED LIQUID CHROME — mirror-finish metallic silver skin, hair and clothing, reflecting the room like a mirror. The vegetable shape is unchanged, only the material is chrome.
• MOOLI (white radish) — a woman whose entire head is a single real WHITE RADISH (mooli) — smooth pale ivory-white skin, long and tapering, with big leafy green radish tops sprouting from the crown. Long straight black human hair falling beside the radish. NOT a turnip, NOT a parsnip, NOT a white onion, NOT a daikon stub. Wearing a plain faded cotton saree, worn thin, no jewellery. IN DELIBERATE CONTRAST TO THE CHROME FAMILY: rendered in ordinary MATTE organic material — dull, soft, porous, light-absorbing skin and rough homespun cloth. She casts NO reflection, throws NO highlight, and does not appear in the mirrored floor or in any polished surface.

ACTION (frozen at this instant): Wide shot down the table. Every chrome family member reflects the chandelier — Anaar, Jamun and Shimla throw hot silver highlights onto the marble. Mooli sits between them in faded cotton, a single dull patch in a room made of mirrors.

===== SCENE 10.1 — IMAGE =====
9:16 vertical. Photoreal 3D cinematic animation, Pixar-grade lighting and skin shading, shallow depth of field, film grain. Indian setting. Rich saturated Indian colour palette.

SCENE: a vast marble dining hall at night, long table, blazing candelabra, mirror-polished floor

CHARACTER CONSTRUCTION (applies to every character in frame): each is a NORMAL ADULT HUMAN BODY with a real vegetable as the head. The vegetable forms the skull and face. Real HUMAN HAIR grows on top of the vegetable, and each has HUMAN eyes, HUMAN eyebrows, a HUMAN mouth and human skin-tone blush on the cheeks, set into the vegetable surface. They are NOT wearing masks, NOT costumes, NOT helmets — the vegetable IS the head. Everyone wears real Indian clothing on a real human body with real human hands.

CHARACTERS IN FRAME:
• ANAAR (pomegranate) — a woman whose entire head is a single real POMEGRANATE — deep red, leathery skin, with the distinctive crown-shaped calyx on top. Black human hair coiled into an elaborate bun around the crown. NOT an apple, NOT a tomato, NOT a red ball, NOT a beetroot. Wearing rich silk and gold — an embroidered silk saree with heavy gold jewellery. RENDERED ENTIRELY IN POLISHED LIQUID CHROME — mirror-finish metallic silver skin, hair and clothing, reflecting the room like a mirror. The vegetable shape is unchanged, only the material is chrome.
• JAMUN (black plum (jamun)) — a woman whose entire head is a single real JAMUN (Indian black plum) — deep blackish-purple glossy oval. Grey-streaked black human hair pulled into a tight bun. NOT a grape, NOT a brinjal, NOT a blueberry, NOT an olive. Wearing rich silk and gold — an embroidered silk saree with heavy gold jewellery. RENDERED ENTIRELY IN POLISHED LIQUID CHROME — mirror-finish metallic silver skin, hair and clothing, reflecting the room like a mirror. The vegetable shape is unchanged, only the material is chrome.
• MOOLI (white radish) — a woman whose entire head is a single real WHITE RADISH (mooli) — smooth pale ivory-white skin, long and tapering, with big leafy green radish tops sprouting from the crown. Long straight black human hair falling beside the radish. NOT a turnip, NOT a parsnip, NOT a white onion, NOT a daikon stub. Wearing a plain faded cotton saree, worn thin, no jewellery. IN DELIBERATE CONTRAST TO THE CHROME FAMILY: rendered in ordinary MATTE organic material — dull, soft, porous, light-absorbing skin and rough homespun cloth. She casts NO reflection, throws NO highlight, and does not appear in the mirrored floor or in any polished surface.

ACTION (frozen at this instant): A long marble dining hall, candles blazing. Anaar's chrome hand points a mirror-bright finger across the table at Mooli, whose radish head is dull matte white. Jamun, also chrome, watches, unmoving.

CAMERA: medium wide, slow push in. MOOD: humiliation.

• MOOLI (white radish) — a woman whose entire head is a single real WHITE RADISH (mooli) — smooth pale ivory-white skin, long and tapering, with big leafy green radish tops sprouting from the crown. Long straight black human hair falling beside the radish. NOT a turnip, NOT a parsnip, NOT a white onion, NOT a daikon stub. Wearing a plain faded cotton saree, worn thin, no jewellery. IN DELIBERATE CONTRAST TO THE CHROME FAMILY: rendered in ordinary MATTE organic material — dull, soft, porous, light-absorbing skin and rough homespun cloth. She casts NO reflection, throws NO highlight, and does not appear in the mirrored floor or in any polished surface.

ACTION (frozen at this instant): Mooli stands alone in the huge marble hall, holding the open tin of silver polish in both dull hands. Around her the polished floor mirrors everything except her. She does not move.

CAMERA: wide, very slow pull back, Mooli small in frame. MOOD: unresolved dread.

ABSOLUTELY NO text, no subtitles, no captions, no letters, no numbers, no watermark, no logo and no signage of any kind anywhere in the frame.
